Let me create a clear scoring system that can be implemented in a spreadsheet or quiz software.ðŸ§® COMPLETE QUIZ SCORING FORMULA
Combining Best Practices (Section 2) + Big 5 Qualifying Questions (Section 3)

PART 1: OPERATIONAL MATURITY SCORE (Questions 5-14)
Calculation:
Operational_Score = SUM of Questions 5-14

Where:
- YES = 1.0 point
- SOMETIMES = 0.5 points
- NO = 0.0 points

Maximum: 10 points
Classification:
IF Operational_Score >= 8      â†’ Maturity = "HIGH" (Ready to Scale)
IF Operational_Score >= 4      â†’ Maturity = "MEDIUM" (Needs Optimization)
IF Operational_Score < 4       â†’ Maturity = "LOW" (Chaos Mode)

PART 2: INTENT SCORE (Questions 15-19)
Question 15: Main Goal (Weight: 3 points)
IF Answer = "Save money"           â†’ 3 points
IF Answer = "Focus on sales"       â†’ 3 points
IF Answer = "Increase capacity"    â†’ 2 points
IF Answer = "Other"                â†’ 0 points
Question 16: Main Obstacle (Weight: 1 point)
IF Answer = "Cost"                 â†’ 3 points (price-sensitive but considering)
IF Answer = "Fear of quality"      â†’ 2 points (needs proof)
IF Answer = "Don't know what"      â†’ 1 point (needs education)
IF Answer = "Lack of processes"    â†’ 1 point (needs consulting)
Question 17: Hours to Delegate (Weight: 4 points)
IF Answer = "+40 hours"            â†’ 4 points (Full-Time + possible multiple VAs)
IF Answer = "20-40 hours"          â†’ 3 points (Full-Time VA)
IF Answer = "10-20 hours"          â†’ 2 points (Part-Time VA)
Question 18: Solution Seeking (Weight: 5 points - MOST IMPORTANT)
IF Answer = "Full-Time VA Support"     â†’ 5 points (READY TO BUY)
IF Answer = "Part-Time VA Support"     â†’ 4 points (READY TO BUY)
IF Answer = "Process consulting"       â†’ 2 points (Considering)
IF Answer = "Just guidance/info"       â†’ 0 points (Researching)
Question 19: Open Box (Qualitative - Manual Review)
Scan for keywords:
- "urgent", "ASAP", "immediately"     â†’ +2 bonus points
- "budget of $X", specific dollar     â†’ +2 bonus points
- "tried before", "didn't work"       â†’ +1 point (objection to address)
- "just looking", "not sure"          â†’ -1 point
Intent Score Calculation:
Intent_Score = Q15_points + Q16_points + Q17_points + Q18_points + Q19_bonus

Maximum: 15 points (without Q19 = 13 points)
Intent Classification:
IF Intent_Score >= 10      â†’ Intent = "HIGH" (Ready to Buy)
IF Intent_Score >= 5       â†’ Intent = "MEDIUM" (Considering)
IF Intent_Score < 5        â†’ Intent = "LOW" (Researching)

PART 3: URGENCY MODIFIERS (Special Flags)
Urgency Flag 1: Losing Leads
IF Question_9 = "YES"      â†’ Urgency_Flag_1 = TRUE
(They're losing leads due to lack of follow-up)
Urgency Flag 2: Staffing Issues
IF Question_10 = "YES"     â†’ Urgency_Flag_2 = TRUE
(They've experienced turnover/absences)
Combined Urgency Score:
Urgency_Score = 0

IF Urgency_Flag_1 = TRUE   â†’ Urgency_Score +5
IF Urgency_Flag_2 = TRUE   â†’ Urgency_Score +3

IF Urgency_Score >= 5      â†’ Urgency = "CRITICAL"
IF Urgency_Score >= 3      â†’ Urgency = "HIGH"
IF Urgency_Score = 0       â†’ Urgency = "NORMAL"

PART 4: FINAL LEAD PROFILE FORMULA ðŸŽ¯
The Master Formula:
LEAD_PROFILE = FUNCTION(Operational_Score, Intent_Score, Urgency_Score)

// Profile A: HOT LEAD
IF (Operational_Score >= 6 AND Intent_Score >= 10)
OR (Operational_Score >= 4 AND Intent_Score >= 10 AND Urgency_Score >= 5)
    â†’ RETURN "PROFILE A - HOT LEAD"

// Profile B: WARM LEAD  
IF (Operational_Score >= 4 AND Intent_Score >= 5 AND Intent_Score < 10)
OR (Operational_Score >= 6 AND Intent_Score >= 5)
    â†’ RETURN "PROFILE B - WARM LEAD"

// Profile C: COLD BUT URGENT
IF (Operational_Score < 4 AND Urgency_Score >= 5)
OR (Operational_Score < 4 AND Intent_Score >= 8)
    â†’ RETURN "PROFILE C - COLD BUT URGENT"

// Profile D: ICE COLD
IF (Intent_Score < 5 AND Urgency_Score < 3)
    â†’ RETURN "PROFILE D - ICE COLD"

// Default (edge cases)
ELSE
    â†’ RETURN "PROFILE B - WARM LEAD"

SPREADSHEET IMPLEMENTATION ðŸ“Š
Google Sheets Formula (assuming responses in columns):
excel// Cell: OPERATIONAL_SCORE
=COUNTIF(B5:B14,"Yes")*1 + COUNTIF(B5:B14,"Sometimes")*0.5

// Cell: MATURITY_LEVEL
=IF(OPERATIONAL_SCORE>=8,"HIGH",IF(OPERATIONAL_SCORE>=4,"MEDIUM","LOW"))

// Cell: Q15_SCORE
=IF(B15="Save money",3,IF(B15="Focus on sales",3,IF(B15="Increase capacity",2,0)))

// Cell: Q16_SCORE
=IF(B16="Cost",3,IF(B16="Fear of quality",2,1))

// Cell: Q17_SCORE
=IF(B17="+40 hours",4,IF(B17="20-40 hours",3,2))

// Cell: Q18_SCORE
=IF(B18="Full-Time VA Support",5,IF(B18="Part-Time VA Support",4,IF(B18="Process consulting",2,0)))

// Cell: Q19_BONUS (manual review)
=0 (or manually score based on keywords)

// Cell: INTENT_SCORE
=Q15_SCORE + Q16_SCORE + Q17_SCORE + Q18_SCORE + Q19_BONUS

// Cell: INTENT_LEVEL
=IF(INTENT_SCORE>=10,"HIGH",IF(INTENT_SCORE>=5,"MEDIUM","LOW"))

// Cell: URGENCY_SCORE
=IF(B9="Yes",5,0) + IF(B10="Yes",3,0)

// Cell: URGENCY_LEVEL
=IF(URGENCY_SCORE>=5,"CRITICAL",IF(URGENCY_SCORE>=3,"HIGH","NORMAL"))

// Cell: FINAL_PROFILE
=IF(OR(AND(OPERATIONAL_SCORE>=6,INTENT_SCORE>=10),AND(OPERATIONAL_SCORE>=4,INTENT_SCORE>=10,URGENCY_SCORE>=5)),"PROFILE A - HOT LEAD",
IF(OR(AND(OPERATIONAL_SCORE>=4,INTENT_SCORE>=5,INTENT_SCORE<10),AND(OPERATIONAL_SCORE>=6,INTENT_SCORE>=5)),"PROFILE B - WARM LEAD",
IF(OR(AND(OPERATIONAL_SCORE<4,URGENCY_SCORE>=5),AND(OPERATIONAL_SCORE<4,INTENT_SCORE>=8)),"PROFILE C - COLD BUT URGENT",
"PROFILE D - ICE COLD")))

AUTOMATION LOGIC FOR QUIZ SOFTWARE ðŸ’»
For TypeForm, ScoreApp, or Custom Quiz:
javascript// Pseudo-code for automation
function calculateLeadProfile(responses) {
  
  // Part 1: Calculate Operational Score
  let opScore = 0;
  for (let q = 5; q <= 14; q++) {
    if (responses[`q${q}`] === 'Yes') opScore += 1;
    if (responses[`q${q}`] === 'Sometimes') opScore += 0.5;
  }
  
  // Part 2: Calculate Intent Score
  let intentScore = 0;
  intentScore += getQ15Score(responses.q15);
  intentScore += getQ16Score(responses.q16);
  intentScore += getQ17Score(responses.q17);
  intentScore += getQ18Score(responses.q18);
  intentScore += analyzeQ19(responses.q19);
  
  // Part 3: Calculate Urgency
  let urgencyScore = 0;
  if (responses.q9 === 'Yes') urgencyScore += 5;
  if (responses.q10 === 'Yes') urgencyScore += 3;
  
  // Part 4: Determine Profile
  if ((opScore >= 6 && intentScore >= 10) || 
      (opScore >= 4 && intentScore >= 10 && urgencyScore >= 5)) {
    return 'PROFILE_A_HOT';
  }
  else if ((opScore >= 4 && intentScore >= 5 && intentScore < 10) ||
           (opScore >= 6 && intentScore >= 5)) {
    return 'PROFILE_B_WARM';
  }
  else if ((opScore < 4 && urgencyScore >= 5) ||
           (opScore < 4 && intentScore >= 8)) {
    return 'PROFILE_C_COLD_URGENT';
  }
  else {
    return 'PROFILE_D_ICE_COLD';
  }
}

<a name="system-overview"></a>
ðŸŒŠ SYSTEM OVERVIEW
What This System Does:
This quiz is a self-qualifying lead funnel that:
âœ… Qualifies operational readiness (Can they successfully work with a VA?)
âœ… Measures buying intent (How close are they to purchasing?)
âœ… Detects urgency signals (Do they need help NOW?)
âœ… Segments automatically into 4 profiles (A, B, C, D)
âœ… Personalizes follow-up content (Different message for each profile)
âœ… Optimizes sales time (Only hot leads get calls)
The Magic:
NOT all leads go to sales. The system routes leads intelligently:

ðŸ”¥ Profile A (20%) â†’ Immediate sales call
ðŸŸ¡ Profile B (40%) â†’ Education & nurture
ðŸ”´ Profile C (20%) â†’ Urgency video & rescue plan
â„ï¸ Profile D (20%) â†’ Passive content only

Result: Sales team only talks to people READY to buy ðŸŽ¯

<a name="quiz-structure"></a>
ðŸ“ QUIZ STRUCTURE (3 SECTIONS)
SECTION 1: Contact Information
Purpose: Capture basic lead data
FieldTypePurposeNameText (required)PersonalizationBusiness EmailEmail (required)Results delivery + CRMPhoneTel (optional)Sales follow-upIndustryDropdown (required)Segmentation + customization
Industry options:

Insurance (target market #1)
Real Estate (target market #2)
Small Business / General
Other


SECTION 2: Best Practices (Q5-Q14)
Purpose: Measure OPERATIONAL MATURITY
Question count: 10 questions
Scoring: Yes = 1.0 pt | Sometimes = 0.5 pt | No = 0 pt
Maximum score: 10 points
What it measures: How ready they are to delegate effectively
Score Interpretation:
ScoreLevelMeaning8-10ðŸŸ¢ Ready to ScaleHas systems, can implement VA in 72 hours4-7ðŸŸ¡ Needs OptimizationSome gaps, needs process help0-3ðŸ”´ Chaos ModeNo systems, high friction onboarding

SECTION 3: Big 5 Qualifiers (Q15-Q19)
Purpose: Measure PURCHASE INTENT & URGENCY
Question count: 5 questions
Scoring: Variable by question (0-5 points each)
Maximum score: 15 points
What it measures: How close they are to buying + budget capacity
Score Interpretation:
ScoreLevelMeaning10-15ðŸ”¥ High IntentReady to buy NOW, has budget5-9ðŸŸ¡ Medium IntentConsidering options, needs nurture0-4â„ï¸ Low IntentJust researching, long nurture

<a name="scoring-system"></a>
ðŸŽ¯ SCORING SYSTEM (3 DIMENSIONS)
The quiz measures 3 independent dimensions:

DIMENSION 1: OPERATIONAL MATURITY (0-10 points)
From Questions 5-14
What it measures:

Process documentation
Delegation habits
Cost awareness
Technology readiness
Business systems maturity

Why it matters:

High score = Can implement VA quickly, smooth onboarding
Low score = Will need consulting, higher friction


DIMENSION 2: PURCHASE INTENT (0-15 points)
From Questions 15-19
What it measures:

Main goal/pain point
Solution sought (guidance vs. VA support)
Hours willing to delegate
Budget capacity (implicit)
Objections/obstacles

Why it matters:

High score = Ready to buy, has budget, close now
Low score = Needs education, nurture over time


DIMENSION 3: URGENCY SIGNALS (0-8 points)
From Questions 13, 14, 19 + keyword detection
What it measures:

Active money loss (Q13: wasting 10+ hrs/week)
Pain awareness (Q14: experienced turnover)
Hidden urgency (Q19: "urgent", "ASAP", "drowning")

Why it matters:

High urgency = Move fast, even if low operational score
Normal urgency = Standard sales process

Urgency Points Breakdown:

Q13 = YES: +5 urgency points (wasting $26K/year)
Q14 = YES: +3 urgency points (knows replacement pain)
Q19 keywords: +2 points each ("urgent", "budget of $X", "drowning")


<a name="question-analysis"></a>
ðŸ“Š QUESTION-BY-QUESTION ANALYSIS

Q5: Process Documentation
Question:

Do you have a written manual or process documented for at least 5 repetitive tasks (e.g., email/CRM management)?

Measurement Area: Process Documentation
Answer Options: Yes / Sometimes / No
Scoring:

âœ… YES = 1.0 point
ðŸŸ¡ SOMETIMES = 0.5 points
âŒ NO = 0 points

What It Measures:

Scalability readiness - Can they onboard a VA quickly?
Systems thinking - Do they work ON the business or just IN it?

What It Tells Sales:

YES â†’ Ready to delegate, has foundation. Can start in 72 hours.
NO â†’ Will struggle to train VA. Needs process consulting first OR expect frustrating onboarding.


Q6: Delegation Habit
Question:

Do you actively delegate low-value tasks (e.g., inbox management, data entry) to someone other than yourself?

Measurement Area: Delegation Habit
Answer Options: Yes / Sometimes / No
Scoring:

âœ… YES = 1.0 point
ðŸŸ¡ SOMETIMES = 0.5 points
âŒ NO = 0 points

What It Measures:

Mindset - Are they a control freak or do they trust their team?
Current behavior - Already delegating = easier sell

What It Tells Sales:

YES â†’ Smooth onboarding, knows how to work with support staff
NO â†’ Will need hand-holding + mindset shift. Potential objection: "I can do it faster myself"


Q7: High-Value Focus
Question:

Does your team spend less than 20% of its time on administrative tasks (not related to direct sales or service)?

Measurement Area: High-Value Focus
Answer Options: Yes / Sometimes / No
Scoring:

âœ… YES = 1.0 point
ðŸŸ¡ SOMETIMES = 0.5 points
âŒ NO = 0 points

What It Measures:

Efficiency level - How much time is wasted?
ROI opportunity - More admin time = bigger savings potential

What It Tells Sales:

YES â†’ Already optimized (less ROI but good systems). May need specialized VA.
NO â†’ GOLDMINE - Can save 20+ hours/week immediately. Massive ROI opportunity (30%+ time is admin).


Q8: Workload Measurement
Question:

Do you consistently measure the time it takes you to handle your CRM (e.g., Applied, Nowcerts, QQ) and back-office tasks?

Measurement Area: Workload Measurement
Answer Options: Yes / Sometimes / No
Scoring:

âœ… YES = 1.0 point
ðŸŸ¡ SOMETIMES = 0.5 points
âŒ NO = 0 points

What It Measures:

Data-driven mindset - Do they track or just "feel busy"?
ROI awareness - Can they calculate VA value?

What It Tells Sales:

YES â†’ Will appreciate ROI, easy to show value. Speaks numbers.
NO â†’ Needs education on time = money. Use time-tracking exercise to quantify current cost.


Q9: Cost Awareness
Question:

Have you calculated how much each internal team member costs you (in salary, benefits, and office overhead)?

Measurement Area: Cost Awareness
Answer Options: Yes / Sometimes / No
Scoring:

âœ… YES = 1.0 point
ðŸŸ¡ SOMETIMES = 0.5 points
âŒ NO = 0 points

What It Measures:

Financial sophistication - Do they know their true labor costs?
Buying readiness - Understanding cost = ready to compare options

What It Tells Sales:

YES â†’ Knows $4,500+ per employee is real cost. Will immediately see 70% savings value prop.
NO â†’ Education opportunity - Show them the math: salary + benefits + equipment + PTO + HR costs.


Q10: Sales Management Systems
Question:

Does your team or you have a defined plan for handling and following up on outbound/inbound leads?

Measurement Area: Sales Management
Answer Options: Yes / Sometimes / No
Scoring:

âœ… YES = 1.0 point
ðŸŸ¡ SOMETIMES = 0.5 points
âŒ NO = 0 points

What It Measures:

Business maturity - Are they systematic or chaotic?
Growth readiness - Organized = ready to scale with VA

What It Tells Sales:

YES â†’ Can hand off lead management to VA immediately. Plug-and-play.
NO â†’ Pain point - "You're leaving money on the table daily." Conversion rate opportunity.


Q11: Collaboration Tools
Question:

Do you use any collaboration tools (e.g., Slack, Teams, Asana) to communicate with remote/delegated staff?

Measurement Area: Technology & Collaboration
Answer Options: Yes / Sometimes / No
Scoring:

âœ… YES = 1.0 point
ðŸŸ¡ SOMETIMES = 0.5 points
âŒ NO = 0 points

What It Measures:

Tech readiness - Can they manage remote team?
Remote work comfort - Already working with distributed team?

What It Tells Sales:

YES â†’ Zero friction onboarding VA remotely. Understands remote work.
NO â†’ May need basic tech onboarding (not a dealbreaker). Offer training.


Q12: Insurance-Specific Tasks
Question:

If you are an Insurance Agency: Does any internal team member handle COIs or endorsements regularly?

Measurement Area: Highly Delegable Tasks (Industry Fit)
Answer Options: Yes / Sometimes / No / N/A
Scoring:

âœ… YES = 1.0 point
ðŸŸ¡ SOMETIMES = 0.5 points
âŒ NO = 0 points
âšª N/A = Skip (not insurance)

What It Measures:

Industry fit - Are they in your target market?
Immediate use case - Specific task to delegate NOW

What It Tells Sales:

YES â†’ Perfect fit, immediate ROI. Lead with "We handle 100+ COIs/month for agencies like yours."
NO â†’ Focus on other admin tasks (billing, data entry, customer service).


Q13: Wasted Time (URGENCY FLAG 1) âš ï¸
Question:

Does your team spend more than 10 hours per week on tasks that could be delegated to someone at a lower cost?

Measurement Area: Highly Delegable Tasks (Opportunity Size)
Answer Options: Yes / Sometimes / No
Scoring (REVERSE SCORE!):

âŒ YES = 0 operational points BUT +5 urgency points
ðŸŸ¡ SOMETIMES = 0.5 operational points + 2 urgency points
âœ… NO = 1.0 operational point + 0 urgency points

What It Measures:

Urgency level - Are they actively losing money NOW?
Opportunity cost - Quantifiable loss ($26,000/year wasted)

âš ï¸ CRITICAL NOTE:
This is a REVERSE SCORE question!

YES = Low operational health BUT HIGH urgency to buy
NO = High operational health BUT less immediate pain

What It Tells Sales:

YES â†’ ðŸš¨ CRISIS MODE - "You're losing $26,000/year in wasted time. Let's fix this NOW."
NO â†’ Well-staffed but use other pain points for scaling.

âœ… NO = 1.0 operational point + 0 urgency points

ðŸŸ¡ Increase capacity = 2 points (WARM - growing, needs help)
â„ï¸ Other = 0 points (COLD - exploring, unclear motivation)

ðŸ”„ AUTOMATIC DECISION MATRIX
How the System Routes Leads:
javascript// DECISION LOGIC (Pseudocode)

IF (Operational >= 6 AND Intent >= 10) {
    PROFILE = "A: HOT LEAD"
    ACTION = "Schedule sales call immediately"
    PRIORITY = 1
}

ELSE IF (Operational >= 4 AND Intent >= 10 AND Urgency >= 5) {
    PROFILE = "A: HOT LEAD"
    ACTION = "Schedule sales call immediately"
    PRIORITY = 1
}

ELSE IF (Operational >= 4 AND Intent 5-9) {
    PROFILE = "B: WARM LEAD"
    ACTION = "Send guide + nurture sequence"
    PRIORITY = 2
}

ELSE IF (Operational >= 6 AND Intent >= 5) {
    PROFILE = "B: WARM LEAD"
    ACTION = "Send guide + nurture sequence"
    PRIORITY = 2
}

ELSE IF (Operational < 4 AND Urgency >= 5) {
    PROFILE = "C: COLD BUT URGENT"
    ACTION = "Send urgency video + rescue offer"
    PRIORITY = 3
}

ELSE IF (Operational < 4 AND Intent >= 8) {
    PROFILE = "C: COLD BUT URGENT"
    ACTION = "Send urgency video + rescue offer"
    PRIORITY = 3
}

ELSE {
    PROFILE = "D: ICE COLD"
    ACTION = "Passive nurture only"
    PRIORITY = 4
}

OBJECTION HANDLING BY PROFILE:
Objection: "It's too expensive"
Profile A response:

"I understand budget is a concern. Let me show you the math: Your current team member costs you $4,500/month all-in (salary + benefits + overhead). Our full-time VA is $1,300/month. That's a net savings of $3,200/month or $38,400/year. In what world is saving $38K/year 'too expensive'?"

Profile B response:

"I hear you - budget is important. That's why I sent you the ROI calculator. When you fill it out, you'll see that most of our clients pay for the VA in saved time within 2-3 weeks. Then it's pure profit from there. Have you had a chance to run your numbers yet?"


Objection: "I don't have time to train someone"
Profile A response:

"Great news - since you already have documented processes (you mentioned that in Q5), training takes about 2-4 hours total spread over the first week. Plus, we provide a dedicated onboarding specialist who handles 80% of the initial training. You're just giving them the 20% that's specific to your business."

Profile B/C response:

"That's actually the #1 reason people hesitate - and it's valid. That's why we created the Process Documentation Package. We'll work with you to document your top 5-10 processes FIRST (takes about 2 weeks), THEN bring on the VA. This way, training is plug-and-play. Want to start with that?"


Objection: "How do I know the quality will be good?"
All profiles:

"Quality is our #1 priority. Here's our quality guarantee:
âœ“ Every VA goes through 40+ hours of training before working with clients
âœ“ We provide the first 2 weeks as a trial period - if you're not happy, full refund
âœ“ We have 100+ five-star testimonials from insurance agencies just like yours
âœ“ Dedicated US-based account manager monitors quality weekly
Plus, I can connect you with [specific client in their industry] who was skeptical at first - they're now on their 3rd year with us and have expanded to 3 VAs. Want their contact info?"

            <div class="card">
                <h3>ðŸ”„ Decision Logic (Pseudocode)</h3>
                <div class="code-block">
IF (Operational >= 6 AND Intent >= 10) {
    PROFILE = "A: HOT LEAD"
    ACTION = "Schedule sales call immediately"
    PRIORITY = 1
}

ELSE IF (Operational >= 4 AND Intent >= 10 AND Urgency >= 5) {
    PROFILE = "A: HOT LEAD"
    ACTION = "Schedule sales call immediately"
    PRIORITY = 1
}

ELSE IF (Operational >= 4 AND Intent >= 5 AND Intent <= 9) {
    PROFILE = "B: WARM LEAD"
    ACTION = "Send guide + nurture sequence"
    PRIORITY = 2
}

ELSE IF (Operational < 4 AND Urgency >= 5) {
    PROFILE = "C: COLD BUT URGENT"
    ACTION = "Send urgency video + rescue offer"
    PRIORITY = 3
}

ELSE {
    PROFILE = "D: ICE COLD"
    ACTION = "Passive nurture only"
    PRIORITY = 4
}
                </div>
            </div>

            <div class="card">
                <h3>ðŸŒ³ Visual Decision Tree</h3>

    <script>
        // Smooth scroll for anchor links
        document.querySelectorAll('a[href^="#"]').forEach(anchor => {
            anchor.addEventListener('click', function (e) {
                e.preventDefault();
                const target = document.querySelector(this.getAttribute('href'));
                if (target) {
                    target.scrollIntoView({
                        behavior: 'smooth',
                        block: 'start'
                    });
                }
            });
        });

        // Show/hide back to top button
        window.addEventListener('scroll', function() {
            const backToTop = document.querySelector('.back-to-top');
            if (window.pageYOffset > 300) {
                backToTop.style.display = 'flex';
            } else {
                backToTop.style.display = 'none';
            }
        });
    </script>
